	<body>
		<category name="Item Part Notifier for BL2 Reborn">
			<comment>Built by Ezeith and Kalli.</comment>
			<comment>Big thanks to original author of Part Notifier, FromDarkHell, for letting us adapt the mod for Reborn. </comment>
			<comment>This mod is only intended to be uses when imported in Reborn. It will not work otherwise.</comment>
			<comment>Item Part Notifier lets you identify what parts each and everyone one of your weapons have and display them in the item card. </comment>
			<comment>The specified checkboxes NEED to be checked in order for Item Part Notifier to work.</comment>
			<comment>Green text are positive effects. Red texts are negative effects. Stocks have hidden matching bonuses. Check the wiki for more details.</comment>
			<comment>Pistol sights have hidden matching bonuses. Check the wiki for more details.</comment>
			<comment>If you notice any bugs, report them on the nexus page or directly to Kalli or Ezeith on the BL2 Reborn Discord Server.</comment>
			<comment>NOTE: Pistol accessory: Double / Masher have one of the two effects, depending on the manufacturer. They don't have both.</comment>
			<category name="Which Version of Part Notifier? (SELECT ONE)" MUT="true">
				<comment>There are 2 versions of Part Notifier to choose from: Full Part Effects and Limited Part Effects.</comment>
				<comment>Full Part Effects will show you the name of the part on the weapon - It will then show you the effect each part has on the weapon itself</comment>
				<comment>Limited Part Effects will only show you the name of the part on the weapon.</comment>
				<category name="Full Part Effects Listed">
					<comment>This choice will show you the effects that every part has on the weapon.</comment>
					<category name="SMGs" locked="true">
						<category name="SMG Barrels">
							<category name="Bandit Barrel">
								<code profiles="">set GD_Weap_SMG.Barrel.SMG_Barrel_Bandit CustomPresentations (AttributePresentationDefinition'GD_Artifacts.Body.Body_Stockpile:AttributePresentationDefinition_0')</code>
								<code profiles="">set GD_Artifacts.Body.Body_Stockpile:AttributePresentationDefinition_0 Description Barrel: Bandit <br><font color="#18FF14">X2 Bullets, Damage</font> <font color="#FF0505">Accuracy</font></code>
								<code profiles="">set GD_Artifacts.Body.Body_Stockpile:AttributePresentationDefinition_0 BasePriority 13</code>
